**Legend:**
- **Pending**: Requires fix (Mapping or Data Model).

## Won't Fix

The following failures are documented but will not be addressed in this release:

### pools/:pool_id/updates Endpoint

**Affected Tests:**
- `pools/:pool_id/updates metadata mismatch - status field`

**Error:** `status` field mismatch - expected "registered" vs "active"

**Reason:** Not part of endpoints included in scope of work for this release. Will be addressed in open-source effort after delivery date.

**Priority:** Low

---

### pools/:pool_id/metadata Endpoint

**Affected Tests:**
- `pools/:pool_id/metadata offchain metadata - homepage field`

**Error:** `homepage` field has unexpected value format

**Reason:** Not part of endpoints included in scope of work for this release. Will be addressed in open-source effort after delivery date.

**Priority:** Low

---

### pools/:pool_id/history Endpoint

**Affected Tests:**

**Error:** `active_epoch` value mismatch (off by one epoch)

**Reason:** Not part of endpoints included in scope of work for this release. Will be addressed in open-source effort after delivery date.

**Priority:** Low

**Error:** Asset history data and pagination issues

**Reason:** Not part of endpoints included in scope of work for this release. Will be addressed in open-source effort after delivery date.

**Priority:** Low

### assets/policy/:policy_id Endpoint

**Affected Tests:**
- Policy asset listing tests

**Error:** Policy assets listing issues

**Reason:** Not part of endpoints included in scope of work for this release. Will be addressed in open-source effort after delivery date.

**Priority:** Low

---

### Block Slot Leader Format - ShelleyGenesis

**Affected Tests:**
- `blocks/:hash_or_number/next` variants
- `blocks/:hash_or_number/previous` variants  
- `blocks/:hash_or_number/next-previous` variants
- `blocks/:hash_or_number - first blocks`
- `blocks/:hash_or_number - hash - generic boundary`

**Error:** Slot leader format mismatch - tests expect `ShelleyGenesis-<hash>` format

**Reason:** The test expectations for slot leader format are **inconsistent with the official Blockfrost API behavior**. The tests expect a `ShelleyGenesis-<hash>` prefix for certain blocks, but the actual Blockfrost mainnet API returns a different format.

**Example:**
- **Block:** `91d46a67e49c343ac54a774facd49884554a9e04e065571f1984626f6c1ea064`
- **Official Blockfrost API:** `https://cardano-mainnet.blockfrost.io/api/v0/blocks/91d46a67e49c343ac54a774facd49884554a9e04e065571f1984626f6c1ea064`
- **Test Expectation:** `ShelleyGenesis-<hash>` format
- **Actual Blockfrost Response:** Different format (not `ShelleyGenesis`)

**Technical Details:**
- The current Dolos implementation returns pool IDs (`pool1...`) for post-Shelley blocks
- The test suite incorrectly expects `ShelleyGenesis-<hash>` format for certain era transition blocks
- This appears to be a **test data issue** rather than an implementation bug
- The official Blockfrost API does not use the `ShelleyGenesis` prefix for these blocks

**Priority:** Low - Test expectation issue, not implementation bug

---
